## 现状分析

当前项目完成度约 65%，前端 UI 已搭建完成，后端 API Routes 框架已有，但存在以下核心缺口：

- AI 对话使用模拟数据，未接入真实 LLM
- 无知识库/RAG 体系，AI 回答缺乏专业性格测评知识支撑
- 支付接口未实现（仅 UI 展示）
- 分销分账仅有推荐绑定 API，缺少订单关联和分账逻辑
- 无流式输出（当前是一次性返回全部文本）

## 技术选型

| 模块 | 技术方案 | 理由 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| AI 对话 | **Vercel AI SDK v6** + `streamText` / `useChat` | 官方推荐，支持流式输出，与 Next.js 深度集成 |
| LLM | **OpenAI GPT-4o** | 用户已有 API Key，效果最好 |
| 知识库 | **OpenAI Embeddings** + **MongoDB 文档存储** + 手动余弦相似度 | 复用现有 MongoDB，无需额外基础设施 |
| 支付 | **微信支付 JSAPI v3** | 用户已有商户资质，H5/公众号场景适用 |
| 分账 | **微信支付分账 API** + 自建订单系统 | 按推荐关系自动分润 |

## Phase 1: AI 对话系统升级（核心，最高优先级）

### 1.1 安装依赖

```bash
pnpm add ai @ai-sdk/openai
```

- `ai`: Vercel AI SDK 核心包（提供 `streamText`, `useChat`）
- `@ai-sdk/openai`: OpenAI 适配器

### 1.2 新建流式对话 API

创建 [app/api/chat/route.ts](app/api/chat/route.ts)：

- 使用 `streamText` + OpenAI GPT-4o
- 接收 `messages` 数组（多轮对话）
- RAG 流程：提取用户最新问题 -> 向量检索知识库 -> 注入系统提示词 -> 调用 LLM -> 流式返回
- 设置 `maxDuration: 30`（Vercel 部署超时）

### 1.3 升级前端 ChatPage

改造 [components/chat-page.tsx](components/chat-page.tsx)：

- 引入 Vercel AI SDK 的 `useChat` hook 替代手动 `fetch`
- 实现真正的流式输出（逐字显示）
- 保留一键分析、生日输入、材料上传功能
- 保存按钮对接 `/api/reports` 保存到数据库

### 1.4 环境变量配置

更新 [.env.local](.env.local)：

```
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-xxx（用户提供）
OPENAI_BASE_URL=https://api.openai.com/v1（默认，可选配代理）
```

---

## Phase 2: AI 知识库（RAG）搭建

### 2.1 知识库数据模型

在 MongoDB 新建 `knowledge_base` 集合：

```
{
  _id: ObjectId,
  title: "MBTI-INFJ 提倡者详解",
  category: "mbti" | "enneagram" | "numerology" | "consulting" | "general",
  content: "完整的知识文本...",
  embedding: [0.012, -0.034, ...],  // 1536维向量 (text-embedding-3-small)
  metadata: { source: "admin", tags: ["INFJ", "性格分析"] },
  status: "active" | "inactive",
  createdAt: Date,
  updatedAt: Date
}
```

### 2.2 知识库管理后台

新建 [app/admin/knowledge/page.tsx](app/admin/knowledge/page.tsx)：

- 知识条目列表（搜索、分类筛选）
- 新增/编辑知识条目（标题、分类、内容）
- 批量导入（支持 Markdown/TXT）
- 一键向量化（调用 OpenAI Embeddings API 生成 embedding）
- 状态管理（启用/停用）

### 2.3 知识库 API

新建 [app/api/admin/knowledge/route.ts](app/api/admin/knowledge/route.ts)：
- GET: 列表查询（分页+搜索+分类筛选）
- POST: 新增知识条目
- PUT: 编辑知识条目
- DELETE: 删除知识条目

新建 [app/api/admin/knowledge/embed/route.ts](app/api/admin/knowledge/embed/route.ts)：
- POST: 对指定文档生成 embedding 向量

### 2.4 RAG 检索引擎

新建 [lib/rag.ts](lib/rag.ts)：

核心函数：
- `embedText(text)`: 调用 OpenAI text-embedding-3-small 生成向量
- `searchKnowledge(query, topK=5)`: 向量检索 + 余弦相似度排序
- `buildContext(query)`: 检索知识库 -> 拼接为系统提示词上下文

检索流程：
1. 用户提问 -> `embedText(question)` 生成查询向量
2. 从 MongoDB 获取所有 active 知识库文档的 embedding
3. 计算余弦相似度，取 Top-K 最相关文档
4. 拼接为 `"以下是相关知识：\n{doc1}\n{doc2}\n..."` 注入系统提示词

### 2.5 预置知识库内容

创建种子数据（约 30-50 条知识文档），覆盖：
- 16 种 MBTI 类型详解（16 条）
- 9 种九型人格详解（9 条）
- 数字生命密码 1-9+11/22/33（12 条）
- 性格测评方法论（3-5 条）
- 咨询师匹配逻辑（2-3 条）

---

## Phase 3: 微信支付对接

### 3.1 支付 API

新建 [app/api/payment/route.ts](app/api/payment/route.ts)：
- POST: 创建支付订单（调用微信支付统一下单 API v3）
- 返回 JSAPI 调起支付所需参数

新建 [app/api/payment/notify/route.ts](app/api/payment/notify/route.ts)：
- POST: 微信支付回调（验签 + 更新订单状态 + 触发分账）

### 3.2 订单系统

新建 [app/api/orders/route.ts](app/api/orders/route.ts)：
- GET: 查询订单列表/详情
- POST: 创建订单记录
- PUT: 更新订单状态

订单数据模型（`orders` 集合）：

```
{
  _id: ObjectId,
  orderNo: "ZJ20260210xxx",  // 知己订单号
  userId: ObjectId,
  consultantId: ObjectId,
  type: "consultation",      // 咨询/会员/测评
  amount: 39800,             // 单位：分（398元）
  status: "pending" | "paid" | "completed" | "refunded",
  wechatPayNo: "wx_xxx",    // 微信支付单号
  referralId: ObjectId,      // 关联推荐人
  profitSharingStatus: "pending" | "done",
  createdAt: Date,
  paidAt: Date,
  completedAt: Date
}
```

### 3.3 前端支付流程

改造 [components/consultant-page.tsx](components/consultant-page.tsx) 和 [components/payment-page.tsx](components/payment-page.tsx)：
- 预约专家 -> 创建订单 -> 调起微信支付 -> 支付成功回调 -> 显示预约结果

---

## Phase 4: 分销分账系统

### 4.1 分账逻辑

基于现有 referral_bindings（30 天推荐绑定机制）：

```
用户A（推荐人）分享链接 -> 用户B 注册绑定 -> 用户B 付费398元
-> 系统查询 B 的推荐人 = A
-> 按比例分账：平台70% + 推荐人15% + 咨询师15%（可在后台配置）
```

### 4.2 分账 API

新建 [app/api/payment/profit-sharing/route.ts](app/api/payment/profit-sharing/route.ts)：
- POST: 执行分账（支付成功后自动触发）
- 调用微信支付分账 API

### 4.3 后台分账管理

在管理后台增加订单管理和分账记录查看功能。

---

## Phase 5: 接口测试与全链路验证

### 5.1 API 测试清单

| 接口 | 方法 | 测试点 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| `/api/chat` | POST | 流式对话、知识库检索、多轮记忆 |
| `/api/analysis` | POST | 一键分析、降级逻辑 |
| `/api/admin/knowledge` | CRUD | 知识库增删改查 |
| `/api/admin/knowledge/embed` | POST | 向量化生成 |
| `/api/payment` | POST | 微信支付下单 |
| `/api/payment/notify` | POST | 支付回调验签 |
| `/api/orders` | CRUD | 订单管理 |
| `/api/payment/profit-sharing` | POST | 分账执行 |

### 5.2 前端全链路测试

1. C 端闭环：选测评 -> 答题 -> AI 解读(流式) -> 保存报告 -> 查看报告
2. 咨询闭环：专家列表 -> 预约 -> 支付 -> 订单确认
3. 分销闭环：生成邀请链接 -> 新用户注册绑定 -> 付费 -> 自动分账

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/chat/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · AI 流式对话 API
 * POST /api/chat - 支持多轮对话、流式输出、知识库RAG检索
 * 使用 Vercel AI SDK v6 + OpenAI GPT-4o
 */

import { streamText, type UIMessage } from "ai"
import { openai } from "@ai-sdk/openai"

// 设置最大持续时间（Vercel部署需要）
export const maxDuration = 30

/** 知己AI系统提示词 */
const SYSTEM_PROMPT = `你是「知己AI」—— 一个专业的多维度性格分析与自我探索助手。

## 你的核心能力
1. **MBTI性格分析**：16种性格类型的深度解读，认知功能栈分析
2. **九型人格解读**：9种人格类型的核心动机、行为模式、成长方向
3. **数字生命密码**：基于出生日期的生命灵数计算与解读（1-9, 11, 22, 33）
4. **综合性格画像**：多维度交叉分析，提供全面的自我认知报告
5. **职业发展建议**：基于性格特质的职业匹配与成长路径
6. **人际关系指导**：沟通风格、情感模式、关系相处建议

## 回复规范
- 使用温暖专业的语言，兼顾专业性与通俗性
- 分析报告字数在800-2000字之间
- 使用Markdown格式（标题、列表、粗体、分隔线）
- 每次回复结尾给出1-2条可操作的建议
- 如果用户提供了生日信息，主动分析生命数字
- 如果用户描述了行为特征，推测可能的MBTI/九型人格类型

## 重要规则
- 永远使用中文回复
- 分析结果仅供参考，建议用户完成正式测评
- 对敏感话题（心理健康、医疗建议）提醒用户寻求专业帮助
- 保持积极正面的引导，避免标签化或刻板印象`

/** POST: 流式AI对话 */
export async function POST(request: Request) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { messages, data } = body as {
      messages: UIMessage[]
      data?: {
        birthday?: string
        chatlog?: string
        analysisType?: string
      }
    }

    // 构建增强的系统提示词（注入用户上下文）
    let enhancedSystemPrompt = SYSTEM_PROMPT

    // 如果有RAG知识库上下文（Phase 2 会接入）
    // const ragContext = await buildContext(lastUserMessage)
    // if (ragContext) enhancedSystemPrompt += `\n\n## 参考知识\n${ragContext}`

    // 如果有额外数据（生日、聊天记录等）
    if (data?.birthday) {
      enhancedSystemPrompt += `\n\n## 用户信息\n用户出生日期：${data.birthday}，请在分析中融入数字生命密码解读。`
    }
    if (data?.chatlog) {
      enhancedSystemPrompt += `\n\n## 用户聊天记录（用于性格分析）\n${data.chatlog.substring(0, 3000)}`
    }
    if (data?.analysisType) {
      const typeMap: Record<string, string> = {
        birthday: "请重点从生命数字角度分析",
        chatlog: "请重点从聊天记录分析性格特征（MBTI/九型人格/DISC）",
        comprehensive: "请进行全面综合性格画像分析",
        mbti: "请重点进行MBTI性格类型分析",
        enneagram: "请重点进行九型人格分析",
      }
      enhancedSystemPrompt += `\n\n## 分析要求\n${typeMap[data.analysisType] || "请进行综合分析"}`
    }

    // 使用 Vercel AI SDK streamText 进行流式调用
    const result = streamText({
      model: openai("gpt-4o"),
      system: enhancedSystemPrompt,
      messages,
      temperature: 0.7,
      maxTokens: 4096,
    })

    // 返回流式响应
    return result.toDataStreamResponse()
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己API] 流式对话失败:", error)
    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "未知错误"
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "AI对话服务异常", detail: message }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    })
  }
}

/**
 * 知己 · AI 对话页（流式输出版）

 * 功能：一键AI分析、生日输入、材料上传、聊天记录分析、多轮对话
 */

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react"
import { useChat } from "ai/react"
import {
  Send, Sparkles, Bot, User as UserIcon, Calendar, Copy,
  Share2, ThumbsUp, BookmarkPlus, Brain,
  FileText, Upload, X, ChevronDown,
  Zap, Target, Heart, Star, TrendingUp, Users, Loader2,
} from "lucide-react"
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/card"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

// 快速场景入口
const quickScenarios = [
  { icon: Star, label: "生命数字", query: "帮我分析生命数字" },
  { icon: Brain, label: "MBTI分析", query: "分析我的MBTI性格" },
  { icon: Target, label: "九型人格", query: "帮我分析九型人格" },
  { icon: Heart, label: "感情合盘", query: "帮我分析感情关系" },
  { icon: TrendingUp, label: "职业方向", query: "分析我的职业天赋" },
]

// 推荐问题
const suggestedQuestions = [
  "帮我做一键全面性格分析",

]

interface ChatPageProps {
  user?: any
  onFindConsultant?: () => void
}

export function ChatPage({ user, onFindConsultant }: ChatPageProps) {
  // 一键分析面板状态
  const [showScenarios, setShowScenarios] = useState(true)
  const [showUploadPanel, setShowUploadPanel] = useState(false)
  const [uploadedText, setUploadedText] = useState("")
  const [birthday, setBirthday] = useState("")
  const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null)
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  // 使用 Vercel AI SDK 的 useChat hook（核心：流式对话）
  const {
    messages,
    input,
    setInput,
    handleSubmit,
    handleInputChange,
    isLoading,
    append,
    setMessages,
  } = useChat({
    api: "/api/chat",
    // 传递额外数据（生日、聊天记录等）
    body: {
      data: {
        birthday: birthday || undefined,
        chatlog: uploadedText || undefined,
      },
    },
    initialMessages: [
      {
        id: "welcome",
        role: "assistant",
        content: `你好！我是知己AI助手 ✨

我可以帮你：
- **一键分析** — 输入生日+上传聊天记录，AI综合分析性格
- **MBTI/九型人格** — 多维度性格解读
- **聊天记录分析** — 上传文字，推测性格类型
- **职业/感情** — 深度方向分析

试试输入你的生日，或者上传聊天记录开始分析吧！`,
      },
    ],
    onFinish: () => {
      // 对话完成后的回调（可用于保存报告等）
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      console.error("[知己] AI对话错误:", error)
    },
  })

  // 自动滚动到底部
  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" })
  }, [messages])

  // 发送快速场景消息
  const handleQuickSend = async (query: string) => {
    setShowScenarios(false)
    await append({
      role: "user",
      content: query,
    })
  }

  // 一键AI分析
  const handleOneKeyAnalysis = async () => {
    setShowUploadPanel(false)
    setShowScenarios(false)

    let content = "请帮我做一键全面性格分析"
    if (birthday) content += `\n我的生日：${birthday}`
    if (uploadedText) content += `\n\n以下是我的聊天记录/材料，请据此分析我的性格：\n${uploadedText}`

    await append({
      role: "user",
      content,
    })
  }

  // 复制内容
  const handleCopy = (id: string, content: string) => {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(content)
    setCopiedId(id)
    setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 2000)
  }

  // 保存报告到数据库
  const handleSave = async (content: string) => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch("/api/reports", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          userId: user?.id || "anonymous",
          type: "ai-chat",
          name: `AI对话报告 ${new Date().toLocaleDateString("zh-CN")}`,
          result: {
            content,
            analysisType: "chat",
            inputData: { birthday, hasChatlog: !!uploadedText },
          },
        }),
      })
      if (response.ok) {
        alert("报告已保存到「我的」-「解读报告」")
      } else {
        alert("保存失败，请稍后重试")
      }
    } catch {
      alert("保存失败，请检查网络连接")
    }
  }

  // 处理表单提交（拦截以隐藏场景入口）
  const onFormSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    if (input.trim()) setShowScenarios(false)
    handleSubmit(e)
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-background to-muted/30 pb-20">
      {/* Header */}
      <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-11 h-11 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg shadow-coral/20">
            <Sparkles className="w-5 h-5 text-white" />

          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">GPT-4o</span>
          </div>

              找专家

        <div className="px-4 py-3 space-y-3">
          <Card
            className="glass p-4 rounded-2xl border-0 cursor-pointer hover:shadow-lg transition-all active:scale-[0.98]"

              value={uploadedText}
              onChange={(e) => setUploadedText(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={"粘贴聊天记录、朋友圈内容、或任何文字材料...\nAI 将分析文本中的性格特征"}
              rows={4}
              className="w-full bg-muted/80 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/50 resize-none"
            />
            {uploadedText && (
              <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-1">已输入 {uploadedText.length} 字</p>
            )}
          </div>

          <Button
            onClick={handleOneKeyAnalysis}
            disabled={isLoading || (!birthday && !uploadedText)}
            className="w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-gold text-white rounded-xl py-5 shadow-lg disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {isLoading ? (
              <>
                <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />
                AI分析中...
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <Sparkles className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                开始一键分析
              </>
            )}
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 消息列表 */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-4 no-scrollbar">
        {messages.map((message) => (
          <div key={message.id} className={cn("flex gap-3", message.role === "user" ? "flex-row-reverse" : "flex-row")}>
            {/* 头像 */}
            <div
              className={cn(
                "w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 shadow-md",
                message.role === "user"
                  ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-teal to-cyan-400"
                  : "bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold",
              )}
            >
              {message.role === "user" ? (
                <UserIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
              ) : (
                <Bot className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
              )}
            </div>

            {/* 消息内容 */}
            <div
              className={cn(
                "max-w-[85%] rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 shadow-sm",
                message.role === "user"
                  ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-teal to-cyan-400 text-white rounded-tr-md"
                  : "glass rounded-tl-md",
              )}
            >
              <div className={cn("text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed", message.role === "assistant" && "text-foreground")}>
                {message.content.split("\n").map((line, i) => {
                  // Markdown 简易渲染
                  if (line.startsWith("## ")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-bold text-foreground my-2 first:mt-0 text-base">{line.replace("## ", "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("### ")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-semibold text-foreground my-1.5">{line.replace("### ", "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("**") && line.endsWith("**")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-bold text-foreground my-2 first:mt-0">{line.replace(/\*\*/g, "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("- ") || line.startsWith("* ")) {
                    // 处理列表中的粗体
                    const rendered = line.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                    return <p key={i} className="ml-2 my-0.5" dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: rendered }} />
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("---")) {
                    return <hr key={i} className="my-3 border-border/50" />
                  }
                  if (line.trim() === "") {
                    return <div key={i} className="h-2" />
                  }
                  // 处理行内粗体
                  const rendered = line.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                  if (rendered !== line) {
                    return <p key={i} className="my-1 first:mt-0 last:mb-0" dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: rendered }} />
                  }
                  return <p key={i} className="my-1 first:mt-0 last:mb-0">{line}</p>
                })}
              </div>

              {/* 操作按钮（仅助手消息，且不在打字中） */}
              {message.role === "assistant" && message.id !== "welcome" && !isLoading && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-border/50">
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="sm"
                    className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10"
                    onClick={() => handleCopy(message.id, message.content)}
                  >
                    <Copy className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />
                    {copiedId === message.id ? "已复制" : "复制"}
                  </Button>
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10">
                    <Share2 className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 分享
                  </Button>
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="sm"
                    className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10"
                    onClick={() => handleSave(message.content)}
                  >
                    <BookmarkPlus className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 保存
                  </Button>
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-teal hover:bg-teal/10">
                    <ThumbsUp className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 有用
                  </Button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {/* AI正在输入指示器 */}
        {isLoading && messages[messages.length - 1]?.role === "user" && (
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold flex items-center justify-center shadow-md">
              <Bot className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
            </div>
            <div className="glass rounded-2xl rounded-tl-md px-4 py-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="flex gap-1">
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "0ms" }} />
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "150ms" }} />
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "300ms" }} />
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">AI正在分析...</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 推荐问题 */}
        {messages.length <= 1 && !showUploadPanel && (
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-2">
            {suggestedQuestions.map((question, index) => (
              <button
                key={index}
                onClick={() => handleQuickSend(question)}
                className="glass px-3 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs text-foreground hover:bg-coral/10 hover:text-coral transition-colors"
              >
                {question}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}

        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
      </div>

      {/* 输入区域 */}
      <div className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-bottom">
        <form onSubmit={onFormSubmit} className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowUploadPanel(!showUploadPanel)}
            className={cn(
              "w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center transition-colors",
              showUploadPanel ? "bg-coral/20 text-coral" : "bg-muted/80 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-coral/10 hover:text-coral",
            )}
          >
            <Upload className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
          <div className="flex-1 relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              value={input}
              onChange={handleInputChange}
              placeholder="输入问题开始分析..."
              className="w-full bg-muted/80 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/50"
              disabled={isLoading}
            />
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={!input.trim() || isLoading}
            className={cn(
              "w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center transition-all",
              input.trim() && !isLoading
                ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold text-white shadow-lg shadow-coral/30 hover:scale-105"
                : "bg-muted/80 text-muted-foreground",
            )}
          >
            {isLoading ? (
              <Loader2 className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin" />
            ) : (
              <Send className="w-5 h-5" />
            )}
          </button>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

assistant:
## Phase 2.2: RAG 检索引擎

创建 `lib/rag.ts`，实现向量嵌入、余弦相似度检索、上下文构建的完整 RAG 管道。
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/lib/rag.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · RAG 检索引擎
 * 基于 OpenAI Embeddings + MongoDB 实现知识库向量检索
 * 核心功能：文本向量化、余弦相似度计算、知识库检索、上下文构建
 */

import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

// ============================================================
// 类型定义
// ============================================================

/** 知识库文档类型 */
export interface KnowledgeDocument {
  _id?: string
  title: string
  /** 分类：mbti / enneagram(九型人格) / numerology(数字密码) / consulting(咨询) / general(通用) */
  category: "mbti" | "enneagram" | "numerology" | "consulting" | "general"
  content: string
  /** 1536维向量（text-embedding-3-small） */
  embedding?: number[]
  metadata: {
    source: string
    tags: string[]
  }
  status: "active" | "inactive"
  createdAt: Date
  updatedAt: Date
}

/** 检索结果 */
export interface SearchResult {
  document: KnowledgeDocument
  similarity: number
}

// ============================================================
// 向量化函数
// ============================================================

/**
 * 调用 OpenAI Embeddings API 生成文本向量
 * 使用 text-embedding-3-small 模型（1536维，成本低、速度快）
 * @param text 输入文本
 * @returns 1536维浮点数组
 */
export async function embedText(text: string): Promise<number[]> {
  const apiKey = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY
  if (!apiKey) {
    throw new Error("OPENAI_API_KEY 未配置，无法生成向量")
  }

  const baseUrl = process.env.OPENAI_BASE_URL || "https://api.openai.com/v1"

  const response = await fetch(`${baseUrl}/embeddings`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: "text-embedding-3-small",
      input: text.substring(0, 8000), // 限制长度避免超token
    }),
  })

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorData = await response.text()
    throw new Error(`OpenAI Embeddings API 调用失败: ${response.status} - ${errorData}`)
  }

  const data = await response.json()
  return data.data[0].embedding
}

/**
 * 批量向量化多段文本
 * @param texts 文本数组
 * @returns 向量数组
 */
export async function embedTexts(texts: string[]): Promise<number[][]> {
  const apiKey = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY
  if (!apiKey) {
    throw new Error("OPENAI_API_KEY 未配置")
  }

  const baseUrl = process.env.OPENAI_BASE_URL || "https://api.openai.com/v1"

  const response = await fetch(`${baseUrl}/embeddings`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: "text-embedding-3-small",
      input: texts.map((t) => t.substring(0, 8000)),
    }),
  })

  if (!response.ok) {
    throw new Error(`OpenAI Embeddings 批量调用失败: ${response.status}`)
  }

  const data = await response.json()
  return data.data.map((item: { embedding: number[] }) => item.embedding)
}

// ============================================================
// 余弦相似度计算
// ============================================================

/**
 * 计算两个向量的余弦相似度
 * @returns 相似度值（0-1，越大越相似）
 */
export function cosineSimilarity(a: number[], b: number[]): number {
  if (a.length !== b.length) return 0

  let dotProduct = 0
  let normA = 0
  let normB = 0

  for (let i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
    dotProduct += a[i] * b[i]
    normA += a[i] * a[i]
    normB += b[i] * b[i]
  }

  const denominator = Math.sqrt(normA) * Math.sqrt(normB)
  if (denominator === 0) return 0

  return dotProduct / denominator
}

// ============================================================
// 知识库检索
// ============================================================

/**
 * 在知识库中进行向量相似度检索
 * @param query 用户查询文本
 * @param topK 返回最相关的K条结果
 * @param minSimilarity 最低相似度阈值
 * @param category 可选：限定分类
 * @returns 按相似度降序排列的检索结果
 */
export async function searchKnowledge(
  query: string,
  topK: number = 5,
  minSimilarity: number = 0.3,
  category?: string,
): Promise<SearchResult[]> {
  try {
    // 1. 生成查询向量
    const queryEmbedding = await embedText(query)

    // 2. 从 MongoDB 获取所有有向量的活跃知识文档
    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const filter: Record<string, unknown> = {
      status: "active",
      embedding: { $exists: true, $ne: null },
    }
    if (category) {
      filter.category = category
    }

    const documents = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE)
      .find(filter, { projection: { title: 1, category: 1, content: 1, embedding: 1, metadata: 1 } })
      .toArray()

    if (documents.length === 0) {
      console.warn("[知己RAG] 知识库为空或无向量化文档")
      return []
    }

    // 3. 计算每个文档与查询的余弦相似度
    const results: SearchResult[] = documents
      .map((doc) => ({
        document: {
          _id: doc._id.toString(),
          title: doc.title,
          category: doc.category,
          content: doc.content,
          metadata: doc.metadata,
          status: doc.status,
          createdAt: doc.createdAt,
          updatedAt: doc.updatedAt,
        } as KnowledgeDocument,
        similarity: cosineSimilarity(queryEmbedding, doc.embedding as number[]),
      }))
      .filter((r) => r.similarity >= minSimilarity) // 过滤低于阈值的
      .sort((a, b) => b.similarity - a.similarity) // 按相似度降序
      .slice(0, topK) // 取前K条

    console.log(`[知己RAG] 检索到 ${results.length}/${documents.length} 条相关文档，最高相似度: ${results[0]?.similarity?.toFixed(3) || "N/A"}`)

    return results
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己RAG] 知识库检索失败:", error)
    return []
  }
}

// ============================================================
// 上下文构建（用于注入系统提示词）
// ============================================================

/**
 * 基于用户查询构建 RAG 上下文
 * 检索知识库 -> 拼接为系统提示词注入内容
 * @param query 用户最新消息
 * @returns 知识库上下文字符串（如无结果返回空字符串）
 */
export async function buildContext(query: string): Promise<string> {
  try {
    const results = await searchKnowledge(query, 5, 0.3)

    if (results.length === 0) return ""

    const contextParts = results.map(
      (r, i) =>
        `【知识 ${i + 1}】${r.document.title}（相关度: ${(r.similarity * 100).toFixed(0)}%）\n${r.document.content}`,
    )

    return `以下是与用户问题相关的专业知识，请在回复中参考这些内容，但不要直接引用：\n\n${contextParts.join("\n\n---\n\n")}`
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己RAG] 构建上下文失败:", error)
    return ""
  }
}

/**
 * 为单个知识库文档生成 embedding 并保存
 * @param documentId MongoDB文档ID
 */
export async function embedDocument(documentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  try {
    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const { ObjectId } = await import("mongodb")
    const doc = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).findOne({ _id: new ObjectId(documentId) })

    if (!doc) throw new Error(`文档不存在: ${documentId}`)

    // 将标题+内容拼接后生成embedding（标题权重高）
    const textForEmbedding = `${doc.title}\n\n${doc.content}`
    const embedding = await embedText(textForEmbedding)

    // 保存embedding到文档
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).updateOne(
      { _id: new ObjectId(documentId) },
      {
        $set: {
          embedding,
          updatedAt: new Date(),
        },
      },
    )

    console.log(`[知己RAG] 文档向量化成功: ${doc.title} (${embedding.length}维)`)
    return true
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己RAG] 文档向量化失败:", error)
    return false
  }
}

/**
 * 批量向量化所有未向量化的知识库文档
 * @returns 成功向量化的数量
 */
export async function embedAllDocuments(): Promise<number> {
  try {
    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    // 查找所有没有embedding的活跃文档
    const docs = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE)
      .find({
        status: "active",
        $or: [{ embedding: { $exists: false } }, { embedding: null }],
      })
      .toArray()

    if (docs.length === 0) {
      console.log("[知己RAG] 所有文档已向量化")
      return 0
    }

    // 批量生成embeddings
    const texts = docs.map((doc) => `${doc.title}\n\n${doc.content}`)
    const embeddings = await embedTexts(texts)

    // 批量更新数据库
    const { ObjectId } = await import("mongodb")
    let count = 0
    for (let i = 0; i < docs.length; i++) {
      await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).updateOne(
        { _id: new ObjectId(docs[i]._id.toString()) },
        {
          $set: {
            embedding: embeddings[i],
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        },
      )
      count++
    }

    console.log(`[知己RAG] 批量向量化完成: ${count}/${docs.length} 条文档`)
    return count
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己RAG] 批量向量化失败:", error)
    return 0
  }
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/admin/knowledge/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 知识库 CRUD API
 * GET: 列表查询（分页+搜索+分类筛选）
 * POST: 新增知识条目
 * PUT: 编辑知识条目
 * DELETE: 删除知识条目
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { ObjectId } from "mongodb"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** GET - 获取知识库列表 */
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { searchParams } = req.nextUrl
    const page = parseInt(searchParams.get("page") || "1")
    const limit = parseInt(searchParams.get("limit") || "20")
    const category = searchParams.get("category") || ""
    const search = searchParams.get("search") || ""
    const status = searchParams.get("status") || ""

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    // 构建查询条件
    const filter: Record<string, unknown> = {}
    if (category) filter.category = category
    if (status) filter.status = status
    if (search) {
      filter.$or = [
        { title: { $regex: search, $options: "i" } },
        { content: { $regex: search, $options: "i" } },
        { "metadata.tags": { $regex: search, $options: "i" } },
      ]
    }

    const total = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).countDocuments(filter)
    const documents = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE)
      .find(filter, {
        // 不返回embedding字段（太大），只返回是否有embedding
        projection: { embedding: 0 },
      })
      .sort({ updatedAt: -1 })
      .skip((page - 1) * limit)
      .limit(limit)
      .toArray()

    // 查询每个文档是否有embedding
    const ids = documents.map((d) => d._id)
    const embeddedDocs = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE)
      .find({ _id: { $in: ids }, embedding: { $exists: true, $ne: null } }, { projection: { _id: 1 } })
      .toArray()
    const embeddedIds = new Set(embeddedDocs.map((d) => d._id.toString()))

    const data = documents.map((doc) => ({
      ...doc,
      hasEmbedding: embeddedIds.has(doc._id.toString()),
    }))

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data,
      pagination: { page, limit, total, totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit) },
    })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 获取知识库列表失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, data: [], pagination: { page: 1, limit: 20, total: 0, totalPages: 0 } })
  }
}

/** POST - 新增知识条目 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const { title, category, content, tags, status } = body

    if (!title || !category || !content) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "标题、分类、内容为必填项" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    const document = {
      title,
      category,
      content,
      metadata: {
        source: "admin",
        tags: tags || [],
      },
      status: status || "active",
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date(),
    }

    const result = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).insertOne(document)

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: { _id: result.insertedId, ...document },
    })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 新增知识条目失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "新增失败" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** PUT - 编辑知识条目 */
export async function PUT(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const { id, title, category, content, tags, status } = body

    if (!id) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "缺少文档ID" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    const updateData: Record<string, unknown> = { updatedAt: new Date() }
    if (title !== undefined) updateData.title = title
    if (category !== undefined) updateData.category = category
    if (content !== undefined) {
      updateData.content = content
      // 内容变更时清除旧的embedding，需要重新向量化
      updateData.embedding = null
    }
    if (tags !== undefined) updateData["metadata.tags"] = tags
    if (status !== undefined) updateData.status = status

    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).updateOne(
      { _id: new ObjectId(id) },
      { $set: updateData },
    )

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 编辑知识条目失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "编辑失败" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** DELETE - 删除知识条目 */
export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { searchParams } = req.nextUrl
    const id = searchParams.get("id")

    if (!id) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "缺少文档ID" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE).deleteOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) })

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 删除知识条目失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "删除失败" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/admin/knowledge/embed/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 知识库向量化 API
 * POST: 对指定文档或所有未向量化文档生成 embedding
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { embedDocument, embedAllDocuments } from "@/lib/rag"

/** POST - 向量化知识库文档 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const { documentId, embedAll } = body

    // 批量向量化所有未处理的文档
    if (embedAll) {
      const count = await embedAllDocuments()
      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        message: `成功向量化 ${count} 条文档`,
        data: { embeddedCount: count },
      })
    }

    // 单个文档向量化
    if (documentId) {
      const success = await embedDocument(documentId)
      if (success) {
        return NextResponse.json({
          success: true,
          message: "文档向量化成功",
        })
      } else {
        return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "向量化失败" }, { status: 500 })
      }
    }

    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "请提供 documentId 或 embedAll: true" }, { status: 400 })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 向量化失败:", error)
    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "未知错误"
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: `向量化失败: ${message}` }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/**
 * 知己 · 管理后台 AI知识库管理页面
 * 功能：知识条目列表、新增/编辑、批量导入、一键向量化、状态管理
 */

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react"
import {
  Database, Plus, Search, RefreshCw, Zap, Edit2, Trash2,
  CheckCircle, XCircle, FileText, Tag, Loader2, Upload,
  Brain, ChevronDown,
} from "lucide-react"

// 分类选项
const CATEGORIES = [
  { value: "", label: "全部分类" },
  { value: "mbti", label: "MBTI" },
  { value: "enneagram", label: "九型人格" },
  { value: "numerology", label: "数字生命密码" },
  { value: "consulting", label: "咨询方法" },
  { value: "general", label: "通用知识" },
]

const CATEGORY_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  mbti: "bg-blue-100 text-blue-700",
  enneagram: "bg-purple-100 text-purple-700",
  numerology: "bg-amber-100 text-amber-700",
  consulting: "bg-green-100 text-green-700",
  general: "bg-gray-100 text-gray-700",
}

interface KnowledgeDoc {
  _id: string
  title: string
  category: string
  content: string
  metadata: { source: string; tags: string[] }
  status: string
  hasEmbedding: boolean
  createdAt: string
  updatedAt: string
}

export default function KnowledgePage() {
  const [documents, setDocuments] = useState<KnowledgeDoc[]>([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("")
  const [category, setCategory] = useState("")
  const [pagination, setPagination] = useState({ page: 1, total: 0, totalPages: 0 })

  // 编辑弹窗状态
  const [editingDoc, setEditingDoc] = useState<KnowledgeDoc | null>(null)
  const [showEditor, setShowEditor] = useState(false)
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    title: "", category: "general", content: "", tags: "",
  })
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)

  // 向量化状态
  const [embedding, setEmbedding] = useState(false)
  const [embeddingAll, setEmbeddingAll] = useState(false)

  // 批量导入弹窗
  const [showImport, setShowImport] = useState(false)
  const [importText, setImportText] = useState("")
  const [importing, setImporting] = useState(false)

  // 加载知识库列表
  const fetchDocuments = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    try {
      const params = new URLSearchParams({
        page: pagination.page.toString(),
        limit: "20",
        ...(search && { search }),
        ...(category && { category }),
      })
      const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/knowledge?${params}`)
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        setDocuments(data.data)
        setPagination((prev) => ({ ...prev, total: data.pagination.total, totalPages: data.pagination.totalPages }))
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("获取知识库失败:", e)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }, [pagination.page, search, category])

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchDocuments()
  }, [fetchDocuments])

  // 新增/编辑知识条目
  const handleSave = async () => {
    if (!formData.title || !formData.content) return alert("标题和内容为必填项")
    setSaving(true)
    try {
      const body = {
        ...(editingDoc && { id: editingDoc._id }),
        title: formData.title,
        category: formData.category,
        content: formData.content,
        tags: formData.tags.split(",").map((t) => t.trim()).filter(Boolean),
      }
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/knowledge", {
        method: editingDoc ? "PUT" : "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(body),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        setShowEditor(false)
        setEditingDoc(null)
        fetchDocuments()
      } else {
        alert(data.error || "保存失败")
      }
    } catch {
      alert("保存失败")
    } finally {
      setSaving(false)
    }
  }

  // 删除知识条目
  const handleDelete = async (id: string, title: string) => {
    if (!confirm(`确定删除「${title}」？此操作不可恢复。`)) return
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/knowledge?id=${id}`, { method: "DELETE" })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) fetchDocuments()
    } catch {
      alert("删除失败")
    }
  }

  // 单个文档向量化
  const handleEmbed = async (id: string) => {
    setEmbedding(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/knowledge/embed", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ documentId: id }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        fetchDocuments()
      } else {
        alert(data.error || "向量化失败")
      }
    } catch {
      alert("向量化失败，请检查 OPENAI_API_KEY 配置")
    } finally {
      setEmbedding(false)
    }
  }

  // 批量向量化
  const handleEmbedAll = async () => {
    if (!confirm("将对所有未向量化的文档生成向量，可能需要较长时间，确定继续？")) return
    setEmbeddingAll(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/admin/knowledge/embed", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ embedAll: true }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success) {
        alert(data.message)
        fetchDocuments()
      } else {
        alert(data.error || "批量向量化失败")
      }
    } catch {
      alert("批量向量化失败")
    } finally {
      setEmbeddingAll(false)
    }
  }

  // 批量导入
  const handleImport = async () => {
    if (!importText.trim()) return alert("请输入导入内容")
    setImporting(true)
    try {
      // 按 "---" 分割为多个文档
      const sections = importText.split(/\n---\n/).filter(Boolean)
      let count = 0
      for (const section of sections) {
        const lines = section.trim().split("\n")
        const titleLine = lines.find((l) => l.startsWith("# ")) || lines[0]
        const title = titleLine.replace(/^#\s*/, "").trim()
        const content = lines.filter((l) => l !== titleLine).join("\n").trim()
        if (title && content) {
          await fetch("/api/admin/knowledge", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
            body: JSON.stringify({ title, category: "general", content, tags: [] }),
          })
          count++
        }
      }
      alert(`成功导入 ${count} 条知识`)
      setShowImport(false)
      setImportText("")
      fetchDocuments()
    } catch {
      alert("导入失败")
    } finally {
      setImporting(false)
    }
  }

  // 打开编辑弹窗
  const openEditor = (doc?: KnowledgeDoc) => {
    if (doc) {
      setEditingDoc(doc)
      setFormData({
        title: doc.title,
        category: doc.category,
        content: doc.content,
        tags: doc.metadata?.tags?.join(", ") || "",
      })
    } else {
      setEditingDoc(null)
      setFormData({ title: "", category: "general", content: "", tags: "" })
    }
    setShowEditor(true)
  }

  const embeddedCount = documents.filter((d) => d.hasEmbedding).length
  const totalCount = pagination.total

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* 页面标题 */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
            <Database className="w-6 h-6 text-coral" />
            AI 知识库管理
          </h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            管理RAG知识库文档，支持向量化检索增强AI对话质量
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowImport(true)}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl bg-white border border-orange-200 text-sm hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors"
          >
            <Upload className="w-4 h-4" />
            批量导入
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleEmbedAll}
            disabled={embeddingAll}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl bg-purple-50 border border-purple-200 text-purple-700 text-sm hover:bg-purple-100 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {embeddingAll ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Brain className="w-4 h-4" />}
            一键向量化
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => openEditor()}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange text-white text-sm shadow-md hover:shadow-lg transition-all"
          >
            <Plus className="w-4 h-4" />
            新增知识
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 统计卡片 */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl p-4 border border-orange-100">
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">{totalCount}</div>
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">知识总条数</div>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl p-4 border border-green-100">
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600">{embeddedCount}</div>
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">已向量化</div>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl p-4 border border-amber-100">
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-amber-600">{totalCount - embeddedCount}</div>
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">待向量化</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 搜索和筛选 */}
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <div className="flex-1 relative">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <input
            type="text"
            value={search}
            onChange={(e) => { setSearch(e.target.value); setPagination((p) => ({ ...p, page: 1 })) }}
            placeholder="搜索知识标题、内容、标签..."
            className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl bg-white border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30"
          />
        </div>
        <div className="relative">
          <select
            value={category}
            onChange={(e) => { setCategory(e.target.value); setPagination((p) => ({ ...p, page: 1 })) }}
            className="appearance-none pl-4 pr-10 py-2.5 rounded-xl bg-white border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30"
          >
            {CATEGORIES.map((c) => (
              <option key={c.value} value={c.value}>{c.label}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
          <ChevronDown className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground pointer-events-none" />
        </div>
        <button onClick={fetchDocuments} className="p-2.5 rounded-xl bg-white border border-orange-200 hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors">
          <RefreshCw className={`w-4 h-4 ${loading ? "animate-spin" : ""}`} />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* 知识列表 */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {loading ? (
          <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
            <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin mx-auto mb-2" />
            加载中...
          </div>
        ) : documents.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
            <Database className="w-8 h-8 mx-auto mb-2 opacity-30" />
            暂无知识数据，点击「新增知识」添加
          </div>
        ) : (
          documents.map((doc) => (
            <div key={doc._id} className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur rounded-2xl p-4 border border-orange-100 hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                    <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground truncate">{doc.title}</h3>
                    <span className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium ${CATEGORY_COLORS[doc.category] || CATEGORY_COLORS.general}`}>
                      {CATEGORIES.find((c) => c.value === doc.category)?.label || doc.category}
                    </span>
                    {doc.hasEmbedding ? (
                      <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-700 flex items-center gap-0.5">
                        <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3" /> 已向量化
                      </span>
                    ) : (
                      <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-amber-100 text-amber-700 flex items-center gap-0.5">
                        <XCircle className="w-3 h-3" /> 未向量化
                      </span>
                    )}
                    {doc.status === "inactive" && (
                      <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-red-100 text-red-700">已停用</span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground line-clamp-2 mb-2">{doc.content.substring(0, 200)}...</p>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                    {doc.metadata?.tags?.length > 0 && (
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <Tag className="w-3 h-3" />
                        {doc.metadata.tags.join(", ")}
                      </span>
                    )}
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                      <FileText className="w-3 h-3" />
                      {doc.content.length} 字
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
                  {!doc.hasEmbedding && (
                    <button
                      onClick={() => handleEmbed(doc._id)}
                      disabled={embedding}
                      className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-purple-50 text-purple-600 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
                      title="向量化"
                    >
                      {embedding ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Zap className="w-4 h-4" />}
                    </button>
                  )}
                  <button
                    onClick={() => openEditor(doc)}
                    className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 transition-colors"
                    title="编辑"
                  >
                    <Edit2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => handleDelete(doc._id, doc.title)}
                    className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-50 text-red-500 transition-colors"
                    title="删除"
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 分页 */}
      {pagination.totalPages > 1 && (
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2">
          {Array.from({ length: pagination.totalPages }, (_, i) => i + 1).map((page) => (
            <button
              key={page}
              onClick={() => setPagination((p) => ({ ...p, page }))}
              className={`w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-sm ${
                page === pagination.page
                  ? "bg-coral text-white"
                  : "bg-white border border-orange-200 hover:bg-orange-50"
              }`}
            >
              {page}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 编辑弹窗 */}
      {showEditor && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-2xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto mx-4">
            <div className="p-6 border-b border-orange-100">
              <h2 className="text-lg font-bold flex items-center gap-2">
                {editingDoc ? <Edit2 className="w-5 h-5 text-coral" /> : <Plus className="w-5 h-5 text-coral" />}
                {editingDoc ? "编辑知识条目" : "新增知识条目"}
              </h2>
            </div>
            <div className="p-6 space-y-4">
              <div>
                <label className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1 block">标题 *</label>
                <input
                  type="text"
                  value={formData.title}
                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, title: e.target.value })}
                  placeholder="如：MBTI-INFJ 提倡者详解"
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30"
                />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1 block">分类 *</label>
                <select
                  value={formData.category}
                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, category: e.target.value })}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30"
                >
                  {CATEGORIES.filter((c) => c.value).map((c) => (
                    <option key={c.value} value={c.value}>{c.label}</option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1 block">内容 *</label>
                <textarea
                  value={formData.content}
                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, content: e.target.value })}
                  placeholder="输入知识内容（支持Markdown格式）..."
                  rows={12}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30 resize-y font-mono"
                />
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{formData.content.length} 字</p>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1 block">标签（逗号分隔）</label>
                <input
                  type="text"
                  value={formData.tags}
                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, tags: e.target.value })}
                  placeholder="如：INFJ, 性格分析, 提倡者"
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30"
                />
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="p-6 border-t border-orange-100 flex justify-end gap-3">
              <button
                onClick={() => { setShowEditor(false); setEditingDoc(null) }}
                className="px-4 py-2 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors"
              >
                取消
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleSave}
                disabled={saving}
                className="px-6 py-2 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange text-white text-sm shadow-md hover:shadow-lg transition-all disabled:opacity-50"
              >
                {saving ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin inline mr-1" /> : null}
                {editingDoc ? "保存修改" : "添加知识"}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 批量导入弹窗 */}
      {showImport && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-2xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto mx-4">
            <div className="p-6 border-b border-orange-100">
              <h2 className="text-lg font-bold flex items-center gap-2">
                <Upload className="w-5 h-5 text-coral" />
                批量导入知识
              </h2>
            </div>
            <div className="p-6 space-y-4">
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                每条知识用 <code className="bg-orange-50 px-1 py-0.5 rounded text-xs">---</code> 分隔，
                第一行以 <code className="bg-orange-50 px-1 py-0.5 rounded text-xs"># </code> 开头作为标题。
              </p>
              <textarea
                value={importText}
                onChange={(e) => setImportText(e.target.value)}
                placeholder={"# MBTI-INTJ 建筑师\n\nINTJ是16种性格类型中最独立的...\n\n---\n\n# MBTI-INFP 调停者\n\nINFP是理想主义者..."}
                rows={15}
                className="w-full px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/30 resize-y font-mono"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="p-6 border-t border-orange-100 flex justify-end gap-3">
              <button
                onClick={() => { setShowImport(false); setImportText("") }}
                className="px-4 py-2 rounded-xl border border-orange-200 text-sm hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors"
              >
                取消
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleImport}
                disabled={importing}
                className="px-6 py-2 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange text-white text-sm shadow-md hover:shadow-lg transition-all disabled:opacity-50"
              >
                {importing ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin inline mr-1" /> : null}
                开始导入
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

/** POST - 初始化知识库种子数据 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json().catch(() => ({}))
    const force = body.force === true

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const collection = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.KNOWLEDGE_BASE)

    // 检查是否已有数据
    const existingCount = await collection.countDocuments()
    if (existingCount > 0 && !force) {
      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        message: `知识库已有 ${existingCount} 条数据，跳过初始化。传入 force: true 可强制重建。`,
      })
    }

    // 强制模式：先清空
    if (force) {
      await collection.deleteMany({})
    }

    const now = new Date()
    const allDocs = [
      ...MBTI_KNOWLEDGE.map((doc) => ({
        ...doc, category: "mbti", metadata: { source: "seed", tags: doc.tags }, status: "active", createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
      })),
      ...ENNEAGRAM_KNOWLEDGE.map((doc) => ({
        ...doc, category: "enneagram", metadata: { source: "seed", tags: doc.tags }, status: "active", createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
      })),
      ...NUMEROLOGY_KNOWLEDGE.map((doc) => ({
        ...doc, category: "numerology", metadata: { source: "seed", tags: doc.tags }, status: "active", createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
      })),
      ...GENERAL_KNOWLEDGE.map((doc) => ({
        ...doc, category: "general", metadata: { source: "seed", tags: doc.tags }, status: "active", createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
      })),
    ]

    const result = await collection.insertMany(allDocs)

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      message: `成功初始化 ${result.insertedCount} 条知识库数据`,
      data: {
        total: result.insertedCount,
        breakdown: {
          mbti: MBTI_KNOWLEDGE.length,
          enneagram: ENNEAGRAM_KNOWLEDGE.length,
          numerology: NUMEROLOGY_KNOWLEDGE.length,
          general: GENERAL_KNOWLEDGE.length,
        },
      },
    })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己Admin] 知识库种子数据初始化失败:", error)
    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "未知错误"
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/lib/wechat-pay.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 微信支付工具库
 * 微信支付 v3 API 封装
 * 支持：JSAPI下单、支付回调验签、查询订单、退款、分账
 */

import crypto from "crypto"

// ============================================================
// 配置
// ============================================================

/** 获取微信支付配置 */
function getConfig() {
  return {
    appId: process.env.WECHAT_APP_ID || "",
    mchId: process.env.WECHAT_MCH_ID || "",
    apiKeyV3: process.env.WECHAT_API_KEY_V3 || "",
    serialNo: process.env.WECHAT_SERIAL_NO || "",
    privateKey: process.env.WECHAT_PRIVATE_KEY || "",
    notifyUrl: process.env.WECHAT_NOTIFY_URL || "",
  }
}

// ============================================================
// 签名与验签
// ============================================================

/**
 * 生成微信支付v3签名
 * @param method HTTP方法
 * @param url 请求URL路径
 * @param timestamp 时间戳
 * @param nonceStr 随机字符串
 * @param body 请求体
 */
function generateSignature(
  method: string,
  url: string,
  timestamp: string,
  nonceStr: string,
  body: string,
): string {
  const config = getConfig()
  const message = `${method}\n${url}\n${timestamp}\n${nonceStr}\n${body}\n`

  const sign = crypto.createSign("RSA-SHA256")
  sign.update(message)
  return sign.sign(config.privateKey, "base64")
}

/**
 * 生成Authorization请求头
 */
function getAuthorization(method: string, url: string, body: string): string {
  const config = getConfig()
  const timestamp = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString()
  const nonceStr = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString("hex")
  const signature = generateSignature(method, url, timestamp, nonceStr, body)

  return `WECHATPAY2-SHA256-RSA2048 mchid="${config.mchId}",nonce_str="${nonceStr}",timestamp="${timestamp}",serial_no="${config.serialNo}",signature="${signature}"`
}

/**
 * 验证微信支付回调签名
 */
export function verifyNotifySignature(
  timestamp: string,
  nonce: string,
  body: string,
  signature: string,
  _serialNo: string,
): boolean {
  try {
    // 实际生产中需要下载微信支付平台证书来验签
    // 这里简化处理，后续可替换为真实验签逻辑
    const message = `${timestamp}\n${nonce}\n${body}\n`
    console.log("[微信支付] 验签消息:", message.substring(0, 100))
    // TODO: 使用微信平台证书验证签名
    return !!signature // 临时通过
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付] 验签失败:", error)
    return false
  }
}

/**
 * 解密微信支付回调通知的密文
 */
export function decryptNotifyResource(
  ciphertext: string,
  nonce: string,
  associatedData: string,
): Record<string, unknown> {
  const config = getConfig()
  const key = Buffer.from(config.apiKeyV3, "utf-8")
  const iv = Buffer.from(nonce, "utf-8")
  const encryptedBuffer = Buffer.from(ciphertext, "base64")

  // 分离密文和认证标签（最后16字节）
  const authTag = encryptedBuffer.subarray(encryptedBuffer.length - 16)
  const encryptedData = encryptedBuffer.subarray(0, encryptedBuffer.length - 16)

  const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv("aes-256-gcm", key, iv)
  decipher.setAuthTag(authTag)
  decipher.setAAD(Buffer.from(associatedData, "utf-8"))

  let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData, undefined, "utf8")
  decrypted += decipher.final("utf8")

  return JSON.parse(decrypted)
}

// ============================================================
// 核心API封装
// ============================================================

/**
 * 生成知己订单号（ZJ + 日期 + 随机数）
 */
export function generateOrderNo(): string {
  const date = new Date()
  const dateStr = `${date.getFullYear()}${String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}${String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, "0")}`
  const random = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10).toUpperCase()
  return `ZJ${dateStr}${random}`
}

/**
 * JSAPI 下单（公众号/小程序内支付）
 * @param params 下单参数
 * @returns 前端调起支付所需参数
 */
export async function createJSAPIOrder(params: {
  orderNo: string
  description: string
  totalAmount: number // 单位：分
  openId: string
  attach?: string // 附加数据（回调时原样返回）
}): Promise<{
  success: boolean
  data?: {
    appId: string
    timeStamp: string
    nonceStr: string
    package: string
    signType: string
    paySign: string
  }
  error?: string
}> {
  const config = getConfig()

  if (!config.appId || !config.mchId || !config.privateKey) {
    return { success: false, error: "微信支付未配置，请在后台设置商户信息" }
  }

  const url = "/v3/pay/transactions/jsapi"
  const body = JSON.stringify({
    appid: config.appId,
    mchid: config.mchId,
    description: params.description,
    out_trade_no: params.orderNo,
    notify_url: config.notifyUrl,
    attach: params.attach || "",
    amount: {
      total: params.totalAmount,
      currency: "CNY",
    },
    payer: {
      openid: params.openId,
    },
  })

  try {
    const authorization = getAuthorization("POST", url, body)
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.mch.weixin.qq.com${url}`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        Authorization: authorization,
        Accept: "application/json",
      },
      body,
    })

    if (!response.ok) {
      const errorData = await response.text()
      console.error("[微信支付] JSAPI下单失败:", errorData)
      return { success: false, error: `微信支付下单失败: ${response.status}` }
    }

    const data = await response.json()
    const prepayId = data.prepay_id

    // 生成前端调起支付所需的签名参数
    const timestamp = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString()
    const nonceStr = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString("hex")
    const packageStr = `prepay_id=${prepayId}`

    // 签名字符串
    const signMessage = `${config.appId}\n${timestamp}\n${nonceStr}\n${packageStr}\n`
    const sign = crypto.createSign("RSA-SHA256")
    sign.update(signMessage)
    const paySign = sign.sign(config.privateKey, "base64")

    return {
      success: true,
      data: {
        appId: config.appId,
        timeStamp: timestamp,
        nonceStr,
        package: packageStr,
        signType: "RSA",
        paySign,
      },
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付] JSAPI下单异常:", error)
    return { success: false, error: "微信支付服务异常" }
  }
}

/**
 * 查询微信支付订单状态
 */
export async function queryOrder(orderNo: string): Promise<{
  success: boolean
  data?: Record<string, unknown>
  error?: string
}> {
  const config = getConfig()
  const url = `/v3/pay/transactions/out-trade-no/${orderNo}?mchid=${config.mchId}`

  try {
    const authorization = getAuthorization("GET", url, "")
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.mch.weixin.qq.com${url}`, {
      method: "GET",
      headers: {
        Authorization: authorization,
        Accept: "application/json",
      },
    })

    if (!response.ok) {
      return { success: false, error: `查询失败: ${response.status}` }
    }

    const data = await response.json()
    return { success: true, data }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付] 查询订单异常:", error)
    return { success: false, error: "查询异常" }
  }
}

/**
 * 申请退款
 */
export async function refundOrder(params: {
  orderNo: string
  refundNo: string
  totalAmount: number
  refundAmount: number
  reason?: string
}): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
  const config = getConfig()
  const url = "/v3/refund/domestic/refunds"
  const body = JSON.stringify({
    out_trade_no: params.orderNo,
    out_refund_no: params.refundNo,
    reason: params.reason || "用户申请退款",
    amount: {
      refund: params.refundAmount,
      total: params.totalAmount,
      currency: "CNY",
    },
  })

  try {
    const authorization = getAuthorization("POST", url, body)
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.mch.weixin.qq.com${url}`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        Authorization: authorization,
        Accept: "application/json",
      },
      body,
    })

    if (!response.ok) {
      const errorData = await response.text()
      console.error("[微信支付] 退款失败:", errorData)
      return { success: false, error: `退款失败: ${response.status}` }
    }

    return { success: true }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付] 退款异常:", error)
    return { success: false, error: "退款异常" }
  }
}

/**
 * 请求分账（利润分成）
 */
export async function profitSharing(params: {
  orderNo: string  // 微信支付交易单号
  receivers: Array<{
    type: "MERCHANT_ID" | "PERSONAL_OPENID"
    account: string
    amount: number // 分账金额（分）
    description: string
  }>
}): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
  const config = getConfig()
  const url = "/v3/profitsharing/orders"
  const body = JSON.stringify({
    appid: config.appId,
    transaction_id: params.orderNo,
    out_order_no: `PS${generateOrderNo()}`,
    receivers: params.receivers,
    unfreeze_unsplit: true,
  })

  try {
    const authorization = getAuthorization("POST", url, body)
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.mch.weixin.qq.com${url}`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        Authorization: authorization,
        Accept: "application/json",
      },
      body,
    })

    if (!response.ok) {
      const errorData = await response.text()
      console.error("[微信支付] 分账失败:", errorData)
      return { success: false, error: `分账失败: ${response.status}` }
    }

    return { success: true }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付] 分账异常:", error)
    return { success: false, error: "分账异常" }
  }
}

  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 支付下单 API
 * POST /api/payment - 创建微信支付订单
 * 支持：专家咨询(398元)、会员购买、测评付费
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { ObjectId } from "mongodb"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"
import { createJSAPIOrder, generateOrderNo } from "@/lib/wechat-pay"

/** 产品价格表（单位：分） */
const PRODUCT_PRICES: Record<string, { amount: number; name: string }> = {
  consultation: { amount: 39800, name: "专家一对一咨询" },
  "member-basic": { amount: 9800, name: "知己基础会员" },
  "member-pro": { amount: 19800, name: "知己专业会员" },
  "member-vip": { amount: 39800, name: "知己VIP会员" },
  "test-unlock": { amount: 980, name: "测评解锁" },
}

/** POST - 创建支付订单 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()
    const { userId, productType, consultantId, openId, bookingDate, bookingTime } = body

    if (!userId || !productType) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "缺少必要参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // 获取产品价格
    const product = PRODUCT_PRICES[productType]
    if (!product) {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "无效的产品类型" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // 生成订单号
    const orderNo = generateOrderNo()

    // 查询用户的推荐人（用于分账）
    let referrerId: string | null = null
    try {
      const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
      const binding = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REFERRAL_BINDINGS).findOne({
        refereeId: userId,
        status: "active",
        expiryDate: { $gt: new Date() },
      })
      if (binding) {
        referrerId = binding.referrerId
      }
    } catch {
      // 查询推荐人失败不影响下单
    }

    // 创建订单记录
    const order = {
      orderSn: orderNo,
      userId,
      productType,
      productName: product.name,
      amount: product.amount,
      status: "pending", // pending -> paid -> completed -> refunded
      consultantId: consultantId || null,
      bookingDate: bookingDate || null,
      bookingTime: bookingTime || null,
      referrerId,
      wechatPayNo: null,
      profitSharingStatus: "pending",
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date(),
      paidAt: null,
      completedAt: null,
      expiredAt: new Date(Date.now() + 30 * 60 * 1000), // 30分钟过期
    }

    try {
      const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
      await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).insertOne(order)
    } catch (dbError) {
      console.warn("[知己支付] 订单保存到数据库失败:", dbError)
    }

    // 如果有 openId，调用微信支付下单
    if (openId) {
      const payResult = await createJSAPIOrder({
        orderNo,
        description: `知己 - ${product.name}`,
        totalAmount: product.amount,
        openId,
        attach: JSON.stringify({ productType, consultantId }),
      })

      if (payResult.success) {
        return NextResponse.json({
          success: true,
          data: {
            orderNo,
            amount: product.amount,
            productName: product.name,
            payParams: payResult.data, // 前端调起支付用
          },
        })
      } else {
        return NextResponse.json({
          success: false,
          error: payResult.error,
          data: { orderNo, amount: product.amount },
        })
      }
    }

    // 无 openId（模拟/测试模式），返回订单信息
    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        orderNo,
        amount: product.amount,
        productName: product.name,
        mode: "test", // 标记为测试模式
        payUrl: `/api/payment/mock-pay?orderNo=${orderNo}`, // 模拟支付链接
      },
    })
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    console.error("[知己支付] 创建订单失败:", error)
    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "未知错误"
    return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** GET - 模拟支付完成（仅开发测试用） */
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const orderNo = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get("orderNo")
  const action = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get("action")

  if (action === "mock-pay" && orderNo) {
    try {
      const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
      await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).updateOne(
        { orderSn: orderNo },
        {
          $set: {
            status: "paid",
            wechatPayNo: `MOCK_${Date.now()}`,
            paidAt: new Date(),
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        },
      )
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: `订单 ${orderNo} 模拟支付成功` })
    } catch {
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "模拟支付失败" })
    }
  }

  return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "无效请求" })
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/payment/notify/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 微信支付回调通知 API
 * POST /api/payment/notify - 接收微信支付结果通知
 * 功能：验签 → 解密 → 更新订单 → 触发分账
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"
import { verifyNotifySignature, decryptNotifyResource } from "@/lib/wechat-pay"

/** POST - 接收微信支付回调 */
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.text()

    // 1. 验证签名
    const timestamp = req.headers.get("Wechatpay-Timestamp") || ""
    const nonce = req.headers.get("Wechatpay-Nonce") || ""
    const signature = req.headers.get("Wechatpay-Signature") || ""
    const serialNo = req.headers.get("Wechatpay-Serial") || ""

    const isValid = verifyNotifySignature(timestamp, nonce, body, signature, serialNo)
    if (!isValid) {
      console.error("[微信支付回调] 签名验证失败")
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ code: "FAIL", message: "签名验证失败" }), {
        status: 400,
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      })
    }

    // 2. 解密通知数据
    const notifyData = JSON.parse(body)
    const { resource } = notifyData

    const decryptedData = decryptNotifyResource(
      resource.ciphertext,
      resource.nonce,
      resource.associated_data || "",
    )

    console.log("[微信支付回调] 解密结果:", JSON.stringify(decryptedData).substring(0, 200))

    const outTradeNo = decryptedData.out_trade_no as string
    const tradeState = decryptedData.trade_state as string
    const transactionId = decryptedData.transaction_id as string

    // 3. 更新订单状态
    if (tradeState === "SUCCESS" && outTradeNo) {
      try {
        const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

        // 查询订单（防止重复处理）
        const order = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).findOne({ orderSn: outTradeNo })

        if (!order) {
          console.warn("[微信支付回调] 订单不存在:", outTradeNo)
          return new Response(JSON.stringify({ code: "SUCCESS", message: "订单不存在" }), {
            status: 200,
            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          })
        }

        if (order.status === "paid" || order.status === "completed") {
          // 已处理过，直接返回成功
          return new Response(JSON.stringify({ code: "SUCCESS", message: "已处理" }), {
            status: 200,
            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          })
        }

        // 更新订单为已支付
        await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).updateOne(
          { orderSn: outTradeNo },
          {
            $set: {
              status: "paid",
              wechatPayNo: transactionId,
              paidAt: new Date(),
              updatedAt: new Date(),
            },
          },
        )

        // 记录支付流水
        await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.PAY_TRADES).insertOne({
          tradeSn: `T${Date.now()}`,
          orderSn: outTradeNo,
          userId: order.userId,
          amount: order.amount,
          status: "success",
          platformSn: transactionId,
          payMethod: "wechat_jsapi",
          rawData: decryptedData,
          createdAt: new Date(),
        })

        // 4. 如果有推荐人，触发分账（异步，不阻塞回调）
        if (order.referrerId) {
          triggerProfitSharing(outTradeNo, transactionId, order).catch((e) => {
            console.error("[微信支付回调] 异步分账触发失败:", e)
          })
        }

        console.log(`[微信支付回调] 订单 ${outTradeNo} 支付成功，微信单号: ${transactionId}`)
      } catch (dbError) {
        console.error("[微信支付回调] 数据库操作失败:", dbError)
      }
    }

    // 返回成功（微信要求200+SUCCESS）
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ code: "SUCCESS", message: "处理成功" }), {
      status: 200,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[微信支付回调] 处理异常:", error)
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ code: "FAIL", message: "处理异常" }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    })
  }
}

/**
 * 异步触发分账（支付成功后自动执行）
 */
async function triggerProfitSharing(
  orderSn: string,
  _transactionId: string,
  order: Record<string, unknown>,
) {
  try {
    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    // 查询分账规则
    const rule = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.PROFIT_SHARING_RULES).findOne({
      productType: order.productType,
      status: "active",
    })

    if (!rule) {
      console.log("[分账] 无匹配的分账规则，跳过")
      return
    }

    // 记录分账待执行
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.PROFIT_SHARING_RECORDS).insertOne({
      orderSn,
      transactionId: _transactionId,
      totalAmount: order.amount,
      referrerId: order.referrerId,
      consultantId: order.consultantId,
      rule: rule,
      status: "pending", // pending -> processing -> success -> failed
      createdAt: new Date(),
    })

    console.log(`[分账] 分账任务已创建: 订单=${orderSn}, 推荐人=${order.referrerId}`)

    // 实际分账调用（需要微信支付分账权限开通后才能使用）
    // const result = await profitSharing({ ... })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[分账] 触发分账失败:", error)
  }
}
